Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user reported critical bugs with single-step mode in the UKB workflow visualization:
   - Single-step mode auto-deactivates after a few seconds (unwanted behavior)
   - Graph visualization doesn't show the paused state (shows "Completed" instead)
   - Sidebar content not synchronized with the graph state
   
   User explicitly demanded: "ultrathink. use serena to understand the code. fix it once and for all!!!!!"

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Single-step debugging mode for workflow execution
   - Progress file polling mechanism (`workflow-progress.json`)
   - Race condition handling in file read/write operations
   - Status state machine: pending → running → completed/failed/skipped → NEW: paused
   - STEP_TO_AGENT mapping for workflow step to agent ID translation
   - React component state synchronization with backend
   - TypeScript union types for status enumerations

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/agents/coordinator.ts`**
     - Contains `checkSingleStepPause()` - the core single-step pause logic
     - **ROOT CAUSE BUG**: The old catch block swallowed all errors and let workflow continue
     - **Fix**: Separated initialization try-catch from polling loop, added retry logic for transient errors
     
     Original problematic code (lines 540-546):
     ```typescript
     } catch (error) {
       if (error instanceof Error && error.message.includes('WORKFLOW_CANCELLED')) {
         throw error; // Re-throw cancellation errors
       }
       log(`Single-step pause check failed: ${error}`, 'warning');
       // Don't block workflow on single-step mode errors  <-- THIS WAS THE BUG
     }
     ```
     
     New robust implementation:
     ```typescript
     private async checkSingleStepPause(stepName: string): Promise<void> {
       const progressPath = `${this.repositoryPath}/.data/workflow-progress.json`;

       // Initial setup - these errors should NOT cause workflow to continue
       try {
         if (!fs.existsSync(progressPath)) return;
         const progress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(progressPath, 'utf8'));
         if (!progress.singleStepMode) return;
         log(`Single-step mode: Pausing after step '${stepName}'`, 'info');
         progress.stepPaused = true;
         progress.pausedAtStep = stepName;
         progress.pausedAt = new Date().toISOString();
         fs.writeFileSync(progressPath, JSON.stringify(progress, null, 2));
       } catch (initError) {
         log(`Single-step mode: Initial file access failed, skipping pause: ${initError}`, 'warning');
         return;
       }

       const pollIntervalMs = 500;
       let lastLogTime = Date.now();
       const logIntervalMs = 5 * 60 * 1000;
       let consecutiveReadErrors = 0;
       const maxConsecutiveErrors = 10; // Allow up to 5 seconds of transient errors

       while (true) {
         if (this.isWorkflowCancelled()) {
           log('Workflow cancelled while paused', 'warning');
           throw new Error(`WORKFLOW_CANCELLED: paused at ${stepName}`);
         }

         let currentProgress: Record<string, any>;
         try {
           currentProgress = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(progressPath, 'utf8'));
           consecutiveReadErrors = 0;
         } catch (readError) {
           consecutiveReadErrors++;
           if (consecutiveReadErrors >= maxConsecutiveErrors) {
             log(`Single-step mode: ${maxConsecutiveErrors} consecutive file read errors, aborting pause`, 'error', {
               stepName,
               lastError: readError instanceof Error ? readError.message : String(readError)
             });
             return;
           }
           log(`Single-step mode: Transient file read error (${consecutiveReadErrors}/${maxConsecutiveErrors}), retrying...`, 'debug');
           await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));
           continue;
         }

         if (!currentProgress.singleStepMode) {
           log('Single-step mode disabled, resuming workflow', 'info');
           return;
         }
         if (!currentProgress.stepPaused) {
           log(`Single-step mode: Advancing from step '${stepName}'`, 'info');
           return;
         }
         if (Date.now() - lastLogTime > logIntervalMs) {
           log(`Single-step mode: Still paused at step '${stepName}', waiting for user action...`, 'info');
           lastLogTime = Date.now();
         }
         await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, pollIntervalMs));
       }
     }
     ```

   - **`integrations/system-health-dashboard/src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx`**
     - Main visualization component for UKB workflows
     - Multiple updates to add 'paused' status support:
     
     **ProcessInfo interface** (added paused fields):
     ```typescript
     interface ProcessInfo {
       // ... existing fields ...
       // Single-step debugging mode state
       stepPaused?: boolean
       pausedAtStep?: string | null
       // ... rest of fields ...
     }
     ```
     
     **getNodeStatus function** (added paused detection):
     ```typescript
     const getNodeStatus = (agentId: string): 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'skipped' | 'paused' => {
       // Check if this agent's step is currently paused in single-step mode
       if (process.stepPaused && process.pausedAtStep) {
         const pausedAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.pausedAtStep] || process.pausedAtStep
         if (pausedAgentId === agentId) {
           return 'paused'
         }
       }
       const stepInfo = stepStatusMap[agentId]
       if (stepInfo) return stepInfo.status
       const isWorkflowComplete = process.completedSteps >= process.totalSteps && process.totalSteps > 0
       return isWorkflowComplete ? 'skipped' : 'pending'
     }
     ```
     
     **getNodeColors function** (added amber color for paused):
     ```typescript
     case 'paused':
       // AMBER with bold outline - clearly shows single-step mode pause state
       return { fill: '#92400e', stroke: '#f59e0b', textColor: '#ffffff', strokeWidth: 4 }
     ```
     
     **getStatusIcon function** (added paused icon):
     ```typescript
     case 'paused':
       return <StopCircle className="h-3 w-3 text-amber-500 animate-pulse" />
     ```
     
     **Both getStatusBadge functions** (added paused badge):
     ```typescript
     case 'paused':
       return <Badge className="bg-amber-500 animate-pulse">Paused</Badge>
     ```
     
     **getInferredStatus in AgentSidebar** (added paused check):
     ```typescript
     const getInferredStatus = (): 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'skipped' | 'paused' => {
       if (process.stepPaused && process.pausedAtStep) {
         const pausedAgentId = STEP_TO_AGENT[process.pausedAtStep] || process.pausedAtStep
         if (pausedAgentId === agentId) {
           return 'paused'
         }
       }
       // ... rest of function ...
     }
     ```
     
     **Status text color styling** (added amber for paused):
     ```typescript
     inferredStatus === 'paused' ? 'text-amber-600 font-medium animate-pulse' :
     ```
     
     **StepResultSummary function type and message**:
     ```typescript
     status?: 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed' | 'skipped' | 'paused';
     // ...
     if (status === 'paused') {
       return '⏸️ Paused in single-step mode (click Step to continue)'
     }
     ```

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **TypeScript Error TS2322**: `Type '"paused"' is not assignable to type '"running" | "pending" | "completed" | "failed" | "skipped" | undefined'`
     - Location: `src/components/ukb-workflow-graph.tsx(3397,113)`
     - Cause: `StepResultSummary` component's `status` prop type didn't include 'paused'
     - Fix: Updated the type union to include 'paused' and added a message for paused state

5. Problem Solving:
   - **Root cause identified**: The old `checkSingleStepPause` catch block swallowed ALL errors (including transient file read errors during polling) and allowed the workflow to continue. This meant any momentary file access issue would break single-step mode.
   - **Solution**: Separated error handling - initial setup errors skip pause gracefully, but polling errors retry up to 10 times (5 seconds) before giving up
   - **Graph sync issue**: The frontend `getNodeStatus` didn't check for paused state at all - it only returned the 5 standard statuses
   - **Sidebar sync issue**: Same problem in `getInferredStatus` function in AgentSidebar component

6. All user messages:
   - `/sl` - Read session logs for continuity
   - `ukb full` - Run complete UKB analysis workflow
   - `am in single-step mode and should be on Observation Creation... but the graph doesn't show this. After a few seconds, the single-step mode is deactivated (automatically - unwanted behavior!!) and the WF continues. Trace and debug this. This is getting tedious. ### Read - 2026-01-13 16:06:57 UTC [17:06:57 CEST]

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree → nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/2026-01-13_1700-1800_g9b30a.md",
  "limit": 500
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```

     3→**Generated:** 2026-01-13T16:00:07.624Z

2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t

   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree → nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`

- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory

- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed
